 <div class="col-lg-8">
 <div class="post-content style-light double-bottom-padding"><br><a
 href="https://www.blogtalkradio.com/lifecoachradionetwork/2019/01/25/free-the-hamster-the-4-stages-of-career-reinvention.mp3"
 target="_blank"></a><br><audio controls=""
 src="https://www.blogtalkradio.com/lifecoachradionetwork/2019/01/25/free-the-hamster-the-4-stages-of-career-reinvention.mp3"
 type="audio/mpeg" preload="none"></audio><br><img width="400"
 height="400" src="https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1.jpg"
 class="attachment-large size-large wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy"
 srcset="https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1.jpg 400w,
 https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1-150x150.jpg 150w,
 https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1-300x300.jpg 300w,
 https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1-200x200.jpg 200w,
 https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1-64x64.jpg 64w,

 https://www.oneideaaway.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/LCRNs-logo-new-1-125x125.jpg 125w" sizes="(max-width:
 400px) 100vw, 400px"><p>Free The Hamster&nbsp;is a show about career change, transition, reinvention,
 and dealing with the fear of leaping into the unknown.&nbsp;Have you hit a wall with your career? Are you asking
 yourself Why am I doing what Im doing? Perhaps career reinvention is for you.</p>
 <p>This Episode:&nbsp;In order to reinvent ones career, I have identified, what I think, are 4 essential
 stages.</p>
 <p>Harry Prichett: Ive integrated my experiences as an actor, writer, improviser, and communicator to establish
 a career as a certified professional coach.&nbsp;Building on extensive research, and my own experience with
 reinvention, I have developed a four-stage program to help others launch meaningful and fulfilling careers.&nbsp;I
 use the listening skills I developed as an improviser and the creative problem-solving techniques I learned as a
 producer to work with a wide range of individualssurgeons, television executives, real estate brokers,
 entrepreneurswho are looking for new opportunities.&nbsp;I&nbsp;partner with them to clarify their current
 career issues, identify their challenges and help them discover creative possibilities for the next chapter of their
 lives.</p>
